ğŸ§© Concept

So far:
G_{eff} = G_P G_{norm} \Lambda^{G_{exp}} (1 + \eta S)
was too suppressed â€” Î›â°Â·Â² is â‰ˆ 10â»Â¹â°â° scale, killing the value.

Now, we augment it with a dimensional bridge term:
G_{eff} = G_P \, G_{norm} \, \Lambda^{G_{exp}} \, \Xi^{\beta},
where:
	â€¢	\Xi = R_q / R_c â€” curvature ratio between quantum scale (Planck length) and cosmic scale (Î› curvature radius),
	â€¢	\beta â€” tunable bridge exponent,
	â€¢	R_q = \sqrt{ \hbar G_P / c^3 },
	â€¢	R_c = \sqrt{3 / \Lambda}.

This term reconnects microscopic curvature (Planck regime) with the cosmic curvature (vacuum Î›).
If correct, there will be a narrow Î²-window where G_{eff} â‰ˆ G_P.
